Release Notes for

STM32CubeWB Firmware Package

Copyright © 2019 STMicroelectronics

Purpose

STM32Cube is an STMicroelectronics original initiative to ease developers life by reducing development efforts, time and cost.

STM32Cube covers STM32 portfolio.

STM32Cube Version 1.x includes:

  • The STM32CubeMX, a graphical software configuration tool that allows to generate C initialization code using graphical wizards.
  • A comprehensive embedded software platform, delivered per series (such as STM32CubeWB for STM32WB series)
    • The STM32Cube HAL, an STM32 abstraction layer embedded software, ensuring maximized portability across STM32 portfolio
    • A consistent set of middleware components such as RTOS, USB, TCP/IP, Graphics, STM32WPAN

All embedded software utilities come with a full set of examples.

The STM32Cube firmware solution offers a straightforward API with a modular architecture, making it simple to fine tune custom applications and scalable to fit most requirements.

The HAL (Hardware Abstraction Layer) & LL (Low Layers) drivers provided within this package supports the following STM32WBxx product:

  • STM32WB55xx
  • STM32WB50xx
  • STM32WB5Mxx
  • STM32WB35xx
  • STM32WB30xx
  • STM32WB15xx
  • STM32WB10xx
  • STM32WB1Mxx

The HAL and LL drivers provided within this package are compliant with MISRA-C®:2012 guidelines, and have been reviewed with a static analysis tool to eliminate possible run-time errors. Reports are available on demand.

For quick getting started with the STM32CubeWB firmware package, refer to UM2550 and you can download firmware updates and all the latest documentation from www.st.com/stm32cubefw

Here is the list of references to user documents:

Update History

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4 and FUS updates

  • BLE updates:
    • TCRL-2025-1 compliancy.
    • New feature added : Randomized RPA Updates. (Core Specification V6.1).
  • 802.15.4 general updates: 
    • Bug fixes.
  • FUS updates:
    • New FUS version : V2.1.0.
    • Safeboot version : V2.0.1.


Maintenance Release for HAL/LL Drivers updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL I2C,SPI,LPTIM , IWDG, RTC, TIM drivers.
      • Update of LL IWDG drivers.
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/USB_Device/CDC_Standalon
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/USB_Device/DFU_Standalone
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/USB_Device/HID_Standalone
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/QSPI/QSPI_ExecuteInPlace
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/QSPI/QSPI_MemoryMapped
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/QSPI/QSPI_ReadWrite_DMA
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/QSPI/QSPI_ReadWrite_IT
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/USB_Device/DFU_Standalone
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/USB_Device/HID_Standalone
    • Refer to release notes for further details

Known Limitations

  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • OpenThread API must not be called within an interrupt context. (FreeRTOS context only)
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.

  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

  • FUS v2.1.0

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.60.3 + ST-Link.
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.38 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components.
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.18.0 (GCC 13) + ST-Link.

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), BLE_Thread, BLE_Zigbee, BLE_LLD, Thread, Zigbee or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/B-WB1M-WPAN1/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE updates

  • FUS updates:
    • New Fus version v2.0.0 dedicated for WB5x and WB3x that mainly covers:
      • Robustness enhancements
      • Pairing/bonding data preservation while FW Upgrade is processed
  • Zigbee updates:
    • Add following missing definition : MSG_M4TOM0_PHY_SET_TX_POWER.

Known Limitations

  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • OpenThread API must not be called within an interrupt context. (FreeRTOS context only)
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.

  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

  • FUS v2.0.0:
    • Coprocessor Binaries installation using CubeProgrammer and STLink interface is currently not supported. As a consequence Coprocessor Binaries can be installed only through the USB interface with CubeProgrammer.

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link.
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.38 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components.
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.16.0 (GCC 12.3) + ST-Link.

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

  • release note for STM32WB5x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates:
    • TCRL-2024-2 compliancy.
  • MAC updates: 
    • Improve memory management to prevent memory leaks on overloaded networks.
    • Review outdated indirect data before releasing buffers sooner.
    • Improve MAC state machine.
  • Thread updates:
    • Assert added in the case of OT command called in ISR context. (FreeRTOS context only)
  • Zigbee updates:
    • Fixing corner case issue related to RoutingRecord for Router and related to ZbStartupPersist and ZbStartupRejoin for EndDevice.


Maintenance Release for HAL/LL Drivers updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL RNG, HSEM, RTC, UART, TIM drivers.
      • Update of LL LPUART drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details

Name Version Release note

Known Limitations

  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • OpenThread API must not be called within an interrupt context. (FreeRTOS context only)
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link.
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.38 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components.
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.16.0 (GCC 12.3) + ST-Link.

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), BLE_Thread, BLE_Zigbee, BLE_LLD, Thread, Zigbee or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/B-WB1M-WPAN1/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates:
    • Update to latest TCRL-2024.1.
    • Several bug fixes on Copro side.
  • MAC updates: 
    • Several minor bug fixes : Remove wrong Rx buffer allocation notification, Panid conflict management regression on V1.19.0 release.
  • Thread updates:
    • OpenThread update to SHA-1: 4a0d6b7b6495a1e4e2e03ab7a4f8baa064df4a6e (June 11th 2024).
  • Zigbee updates:
    • The default size tables have been updated. refer to the wiki linked to the memory for more details. wiki


Maintenance Release for HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL ADC, QSPI, SPI, UART, USB drivers.
      • Update of LL ADC, SPI, USB drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates

    • Add B-WB1M-WPAN1_Example-ARM Example

    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/TouchSensing/TouchSensing_1touchkey/Src/tsl_user.c
      • NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/FreeRTOS/FreeRTOS_Mutexes/Src/stm32wbxx_hal_timebase_tim.c
      • NUCLEO-WB15CC/Examples/HAL/HAL_TimeBase_TIM/Src/stm32wbxx_hal_timebase_tim.c

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Concurrent, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates:
    • A new command ACI_HAL_EAD_ENCRYPT_DECRYPT is added to ease implementation of Encrypted Advertising Data feature.
  • MAC updates: 
    • To reduce the ROM footprint, optional features have been excluded from the MAC RFD configuration.
    • Correct PANID conflict notification that might return wrong channel.
  • Thread updates:
    • Increased speed of Thread commissioning and SRP key exchanges, using PKA HW accelerator when possible.
    • Increased Thread RCP stability, robustness and efficiency.
  • Zigbee updates:
    • Fix startup memory leak issue when using TouchLink.
    • Fixed zcl_send_response issue for loopback Default Response.
  • BLE Thread updates:
    • Corrected a low-power over consumption when BLE advertising is started or stopped during runtime.
    • Corrected a bug that prevented to erase flash during BLE activity.
  • BLE Zigbee updates:
    • Corrected a bug that prevented to erase flash during BLE activity.


Maintenance Release for HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL CRYP, I2C, QSPI, TIM, UART drivers.
      • Update of LL LPUART, TIM drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples_LL/TIM/TIM_PWMOutput.

Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM.
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Lowpower
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate.
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
  • The CubeMX projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/FreeRTOS/FreeRTOS_Mutexes
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/FreeRTOS/FreeRTOS_Mutexes
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/FreeRTOS/FreeRTOS_Semaphore
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/FreeRTOS/FreeRTOS_SemaphoreFromISR
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link.
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.38 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components.
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.15.0 (GCC 12.3) + ST-Link.

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), BLE_Thread, BLE_Zigbee, BLE_LLD, Thread, Zigbee or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/B-WB1M-WPAN1/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE, Thread and Zigbee.

  • BLE updates:

    • Full stack updates for STM32WB5x with respect to:

      • The BLE stack better handles the collision between local GATT client request and remote GATT indication.
      • A new SMP configuration is added to forbid use of peer debug key for Secure Connections
      • While waiting for PKA end of computation CPU2 is now in sleep mode to save power consumption.
  • Zigbee updates:
    • Fix implemented inside the stack to solve an issue when sending unicast messages after restarting from persistence.
  • Thread updates:
    • Bug resolution when using the CLI command that made impossible to send further commands.

Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM.
  • BLE:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/APPLI_BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_LPN : limitation on Led behavior on LPN2.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PRF_NODE: limitation on Led behavior on LPN2.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PROVISIONER: limitation on serial terminal during self-provisioning.
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16.
  • BLE Thread / BLE Zigbee :
    • Flash erase operation cannot be performed with BLE Thread / BLE Zigbee applications.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate.
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_Ota.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/Thread/Thread_Cli_Cmd.
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/Thread/Thread_Cli_Cmd.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_RCP_Cli_Cmd.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.14.0 (native GNU ARM 11.3-2023-10) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • Update Examples and Applications to MDK-ARM (Keil) v5.38.

  • BLE updates:
    • BLE Light stack support 2Mbit TX/RX PHY update.
  • BLE Zigbee updates:
    • Correct an issue in the management of the AES driver when Zigbee is used in concurrency mode with BLE.
  • Thread updates:
    • OT stack update to SHA-1: 8bc25042ba5cde20605eec2a329c0dff575303f4 (07/07/2023).
    • OpenThread Command Line Interface (CLI) moved from M0 to M4 in order to optimize memory footprint on the coprocessor.

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL GPIO, CRYP, I2C, SMBUS, QSPI, CORTEX, TIM, LPTIM drivers.
      • Update of LL UTILS drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example.

Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM.
  • BLE:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/APPLI_BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_LPN : limitation on Led behavior on LPN2.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PRF_NODE: limitation on Led behavior on LPN2.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PROVISIONER: limitation on serial terminal during self-provisioning.
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router.
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16.
  • BLE Thread / BLE Zigbee :
    • Flash erase operation cannot be performed with BLE Thread / BLE Zigbee applications.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate.
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_Ota.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/Thread/Thread_Cli_Cmd.
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/Thread/Thread_Cli_Cmd.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_RCP_Cli_Cmd.
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE.
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.38 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.14.0 (native GNU ARM 11.3-2023-10) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), BLE_Thread, BLE_Zigbee, BLE_LLD, Thread, Zigbee or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/B-WB1M-WPAN1/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE  updates:
    • New GAP commands for extended scan and connection have been created: ACI_GAP_EXT_START_SCAN and ACI_GAP_EXT_CREATE_CONNECTION.
    • New parameter setting SHCI_C2_BLE_INIT_BLE_CORE_5_4 for upgraded QDID and declaration ID of Stack BLE 5.4.
    • The following BLE primitives have been renamed: ACI_HAL_SET_SLAVE_LATENCY, ACI_GAP_SLAVE_SECURITY_REQ and ACI_GAP_SLAVE_SECURITY_INITIATED_EVENT to ACI_HAL_SET_PERIPHERAL_LATENCY, ACI_GAP_PERIPHERAL_SECURITY_REQ and ACI_GAP_PERIPHERAL_SECURITY_INITIATED_EVENT, respectively. Moreover, the event parameters Slave_Latency and Master_Clock_Accuray have been renamed to Latency and Central_Clock_Accuracy, respectively.
  • MAC 802.15.4 / Thread / Zigbee  and concurrent mode updates:
    • Enabling of some PHY features (continuous wave start/stop, rx_start/stop, tx_start, set_channel) in MAC/Thread/Zigbee and concurrent firmware.
    • Improvement of the trace mechanism in order to get M4 log timestamp available on all Thread/Zigbee and concurrent applications.
  • Zigbee  updates:
    • Inter core communication improvement (M4-M0+) on all Zigbee applications making it more robust in very extreme conditions (Environment in which with multiple messages need to be processed at the same time).

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL I2C, SAI, QSPI, TIM, RTC, UART drivers.
      • Update of LL I2C, TIM, RTC drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example

Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM
  • BLE:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC : Use of PLL as system clock is not supported when using standby low power mode and RF.
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/APPLI_BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_LPN : limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PRF_NODE: limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PROVISIONER: limitation on serial terminal during self-provisioning
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router
    • Latest Thread Compliant Platform Certification done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The following MDK-ARM project is not functional:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRate
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
  • The EWARM project is not available for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.11.0 (native GNU ARM 10.3-2021-10 or optional GNU ARM 9-2020-q2-update) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE.

This patch release V1.17.2 has to be installed on top of V1.17.1 patch release (based on V1.17.0).

  • BLE updates:
    • Security improvement.

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee.

  • CKS updates:
    • Security improvement.
  • BLE  updates:
    • Compliancy TCRL-2023-1 with BLE 5.4 certification.
    • New BT SIG Certification: [Declaration ID D063070 / QDID 216169] (https://launchstudio.bluetooth.com/ListingDetails/186628).
  • Zigbee  updates:
    • In case of FreeRTOS Application, a new mutex is now being used to protect the sending of commands to the M0.
  • Thread updates:
    • Thread Compliant Platform Certification done on current version.
  • MAC 802.15.4  updates:
    • Proprietary MAC Pib Attribute has been introduced to let End Device to enter in sleep mode once MacDataPollReq is acknowledged with empty data pending field information.
  • BLE/Zigbee Dynamic updates:
    • Corrected an issue on radio access between BLE and Thread that could cause a freeze in the firmware.

conf V1.6.1 release notes
lpm V1.4.0 release notes
sequencer V1.6.0 release notes
LCD V2.0.2 release notes


Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM
  • BLE:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/APPLI_BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_LPN : limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PRF_NODE: limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PROVISIONER: limitation on serial terminal during self-provisioning
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router
    • Latest Thread Compliant Platform Certification done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification - FFD RFD - done on Cube_FW_WB V1.16
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The following MDK-ARM project is not functional:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRate
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
  • The EWARM project is not available for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following application:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link. Support of ARM Compiler 6 (AC5 like warning) for HAL/LL/BSP drivers and STMicroelectronics Middleware components
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.11.0 (native GNU ARM 10.3-2021-10 or optional GNU ARM 9-2020-q2-update) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • THREAD  updates:
    • SED role is now supported for FTD.
    • SSED role is now supported for FTD and MTD.
    • Improved global stability and robustness.
    • Improved security.
  • Zigbee  updates:
    • Robustness improvement in case of radio noisy environment.
  • BLE  updates:
    • Compliancy TCRL 2022-2.
    • ACI BLE primitives naming alignment to standard.
    • HCI_LE_ENHANCED_CONNECTION_COMPLETE_EVENT is now automatically used instead of HCI_LE_CONNECTION_COMPLETE_EVENT when advertising extensions are used.
    • Additional check on HSE Startup time.
  • MAC 802.15.4  updates:
    • Improvement of radio robustness over heavy overloaded and noisy environment.
  • BLE/MAC Static updates:
    • Improvement of radio robustness over heavy overloaded and noisy environment.
  • BLE/Zigbee Dynamic updates:
    • Bug corrected in Dynamic Concurrent applications to prevent switching from 802.15.4 to BLE while radio is in an incorrect state.

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL CRYP, Generic, I2C, SMBUS, TSC, UART, SPI drivers.
      • Update of LL USB drivers
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Examples/FLASH/FLASH_EraseProgram
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Examples/CRYP/CRYP_DMA
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/CRYP/CRYP_DMA

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

Porting IAR toolChain 9.20.1.

  • THREAD  updates:
    • TxPower API support added.
  • Zigbee  updates:
    • Update default ZB_NWK parameter and add new configuration (ZB_NWK/ZB_APS).
  • BLE  updates:
    • BLE GATT caching and Enhanced ATT supported (certified BLE 5.3 - TCRL 2022-1).
    • Application has now the possibility to have scan operation in background with respect to advertising & Connection slave.
  • MAC 802.15.4  updates:
    • LowPower application optimization.
    • Improve robustness in case of overloaded 802.15.4 network.
  • BLE/MAC Static updates:
    • Improve robustness in case of overloaded 802.15.4 network.
  • BLE/Zigbee Dynamic updates:
    • Improve robustness when switching from BLE to Zigbee.

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL FLASH, Generic, I2C, SAI, TSC, UART drivers.
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Examples/CRYP/CRYP_DMA
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/UART/UART_Print
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/CRYP/CRYP_AESModes
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/CRYP/CRYP_DMA
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/I2C/I2C_TwoBoards_RestartAdvComIT
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/UART/UART_Console
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/UART/UART_Printf
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/UART/UART_Console

Known Limitations

  • Following applications are not supported:
    • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Examples/BSP/BSP_Example/MDK-ARM
  • BLE:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/APPLI_BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_LPN : limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PRF_NODE: limitation on Led behavior on LPN2
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_MESH_LIGHTING_PROVISIONER: limitation on serial terminal during self-provisioning
  • THREAD:
    • Thread FTD all roles are supported excepting Border router
    • Thread MTD all roles are supported excepting Border router and SSED
  • ZIGBEE :
    • Latest Zigbee Compliant Platform Certification done on Cube_FW_WB V1.13.1
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRateThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRateThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServerThreadX
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following applications:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V9.20.1 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.11.0 (native GNU ARM 10.3-2021-10 or optional GNU ARM 9-2020-q2-update) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB5Mxx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx & STM32WB1Mxx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board
  • B-WB1M-WPAN1 board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • THREAD updates:
    • Thread 1.3 ready
    • OT stack updated to SHA-1: 32ac6ddfad2bc196e216c42249c73420542daac0 (July 26th 2022)
  • Zigbee  updates:
    • OTA enhancement (OTA support for multiple download in parallel)
    • Adding new parameters to configure the network layer through ZB_NWK_NIB_ID_SedTimeoutLeaveDuration and ZB_NWK_NIB_ID_AllowLostParentFlag
  • BLE  updates:
    • STM32WB1M module support
    • Some New BLE features supported as Appearance writing

Maintenance Release for Middleware updates

  • Update of USB device Library
  • Update of Touchsensing Library
  • Update of Azure RTOS ThreadX

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • CMSIS Device updates
    • Update CMSIS device to include latest corrections
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL ADC, CRC, EXTI, IRDA, LPTIM, RCC, RTC, SAI, SMARTCARD, TIM, UART, USART, USB and LL ADC, LPTIM, RCC, TIM drivers
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Examples_LL/CRC/CRC_CalculateAndCheck
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples_LL/I2C/I2C_TwoBoards_WakeUpFromStop2_IT_Init
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/I2C/I2C_WakeUpFromStop2
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/PWR/PWR_STOP2_RTC
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples/UART/UART_ReceptionToIdle_CircularDMA
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples_LL/CRC/CRC_CalculateAndCheck
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Examples_LL/CRC/CRC_UserDefinedPolynomial
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/RCC/RCC_ClockConfig
    • Add support of new applications:
      • /B-WB1M-WPAN1/Applications/BLE/BLE_HR_P2PServer

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE and Thread updates

  • General updates:
    • Wireless copro binaries corrected to workaround corner case with FUS v1.2.0 that may impact application using OTA to upgrade the copro wireless firmware.
  • BLE updates:
    • Ability to scan only on selected channels
    • Ability to store Gatt database in NVM upon request.
    • Option provided reducing GATT information size in NVM
    • Ability to synchronize with additional beacon
    • Ability to deactivate SMP blacklist mechanism
  • Thread  updates:
    • Thread 1.1 GRL pre-certification passed for FTD and MTD
    • Thread 1.2 GRL pre-certification passed for FTD only
    • Fix several OT API wrapper issues.

    • This revision is not certified and do not pass 5.2.6 & 5.2.7 GRL test.
  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Client_Router_ThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pClient_Ext
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer_Ext
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Datarate
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_PressMeas_Client_Router
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_PressMeas_Server_Coord
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Server_Coord_FreeRTOS
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Client_Router_FreeRTOS
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following applications:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_ThermometerSensor/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Client_Router/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Server_Coord/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_Model_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE
  • If you face issue to access some files during compilation (e.g. “cannot open source input file”) with some examples on partner IDEs, please consider to move either the full package manually or just the example using the “Example Selector” from STM32CubeMX, closer to the root of the disk (long path issue).

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V8.20.2 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.9.0 (native GNU ARM 10.3-2021-10 or optional GNU ARM 9-2020-q2-update) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx, STM32WB10xx devices
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates:
    • Support BLEv5.3
    • ThreadX OS support
  • Zigbee updates:
    • BDB 3.0.1 & ZCL 8 update
    • Network Leave management update
    • TX power setting of Zigbee before establishing network
    • Manufacturer ID persistence on ZbStartup
    • Multichannel Scan fix
    • Export ZbNlmeEdScanReq on M4 side
    • ThreadX OS support with two new applications (Zigbee_OnOff_ClientRouter_ThreadX)
    • New Zigbee applications (Zigbee_OnOff_ChannelsAgility)
  • Thread  updates:
    • Support Threadv1.1 based on Openthreadv1.2 (commit ec02abc47c6d7663f82132d64555839a5c93e018)
      N.B.: This revision is not certified do not pass 5.2.6 & 5.2.7 GRL test, Please note that SRAM2RST Option Byte must be checked.
      Certifiable solution can be done using FW 1.13.x
    • Provide the choice to customer to handle Thread NVM at application processor level
    • ThreadX OS support​​​​​ (Thread_Coap_Generic_ThreadX)
  • ThreadX-OS middleware
    • Add support of Azure RTOS-ThreadX Middleware, Provide Connectivity examples.

Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • HAL/LL Drivers updates:
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL COMP, EXTI, FLASH, GPIO, I2C, IRDA, LPTIM, PKA, PWR, RCC, SAI, SMARTCARD, TIM, UART, USART and USB drivers
      • HAL code quality enhancement for MISRA-C Rule-8.13 by adding Cont qualifiers
      • Update of LL COMP, I2C, LPTIM, RCC, TIM, UART, USART and USB drivers
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects  updates:
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates
    • Introducing following new binary Full stack extended: stm32wbxx_BLE_Stack_full_extended_fw.bin including BLE extended advertising features.
      • To use this binary on stm32wb5x, it is necessary to adapt the scatter file in the BLE applications (Refer to binaries description above for further details).
    • Introducing following new binary HCI layer extended: stm32wbxx_BLE_HCILayer_extended_fw.bin including BLE extended advertising features.
    • Compared to previous delivery, the binary stm32wbxx_BLE_Stack_full_fw.bin is linked to modified Basic stack library with included Phy update(2Mb/s) and additional beacon.
    • BLE Binaries FWs are compliant to BLE5.2 certified features TCRL2021-1
  • Zigbee updates
    • Fix Manufacturer ID management : Node Descriptor Response Manufacturer ID can be set using ZbApsSet. apsManufacturerId is no more overwritten when calling ZbStartup
  • BLE Zigbee Static updates:
    • Fix memory leak on transition from Zigbee to BLE
    • Following application has been added:
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE_Zigbee/BLE_Zigbee_Static

    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.

Main Changes

Patch Release for BLE, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates
    • Introducing following new binary: stm32wb5x_BLE_Stack_full_extended_fw.bin to support BLE extended advertising (under flag selection with predefined configuration) in addition to previous BLE features already included in binary: stm32wb5x_BLE_Stack_full_fw.bin
  • Zigbee updates
    • Zigbee stack patches in order to solve R22 security vulnerability reported by the CSA (Security Incident Number: 2021-ZP-0401)
  • BLE-Thread Dynamic Concurrent Mode
    • Correct low power consumption issue

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, 802.15.4, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • BLE updates
    • Multi link support
    • L2CAP connection-oriented channels support (IP over BLE enabler)
    • ACI_GAP_START_NAME_DISCOVERY_PROC command is deprecated
  • 802.15.4 general updates (Zigbee, Thread, MAC, PHY)
    • CCA (Clear Channel Assessment) Threshold has been increased
  • Zigbee updates
    • 802_15_4 timer improvement solving several issues relative to the wraparound of this timer
    • MW API prototype renaming
  • Thread updates
    • Fix wrapper issue with UDP receivers
    • RCP build: improved commissioning process robustness
  • MAC 802.15.4 updates
    • Fix unicast data processing after restart from persistence
    • Fix wrong erratic PANID Compression Flag on Beacon Request
    • Reduce MaxBe low level threshold allowing user to change CSMA-CA values
  • BLE-Zigbee Concurrent mode
    • BLE-Zigbee static concurrent mode not supported in this release, will be fixed in the next release. Alternative is to use BLE-Zigbee dynamic concurrent mode
  • Safeboot
    • New binaries added: stm32wb5x_Safeboot_fw.bin, stm32wb3x_Safeboot_fw.bin, stm32wb1x_Safeboot_fw.bin.
    • Safeboot is an independent part of the FUS that manages specifically one case: option bytes corruption.
    • When option bytes are corrupted, the STM32WB hardware forces the boot to Safeboot whatever the running firmware.
    • Safeboot is already present in the FUS and this image allows to update it. Refer to AN5185 for more details.
    • Safeboot upgrade is optional
  • All source files: update disclaimer to add reference to the new license agreement


Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • General updates
    • All source files: update disclaimer to add reference to the new license agreement
    • Add README.md file for GitHub publication
    • Correct English spelling errors and typos
  • CMSIS Device updates
    • Update CMSIS devices drivers for all value lines not supporting SMPS
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL ADC, GPIO, I2C, IRDA, IWDG, LPTIM, PKA, RCC, SMARTCARD, SMBUS, TIM, UART, USB and LL ADC, RCC drivers
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares and alignments with CubeMx
    • Add support of new applications:
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRate_ota
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_MeshLightingLPN
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_MeshLightingPRFNode

Known Limitations

  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.
  • The STM32CubeIDE projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/STM32CubeIDE
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following applications:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_DataThroughput/STM32CubeIDE
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_DataThroughput/STM32CubeIDE
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_ThermometerSensor/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Client_Router/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Server_Coord/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_Model_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE
  • BLE-Thread Dynamic Concurrent Mode : no longer hit 2uA consumption in idle state (1.8mA instead)

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V8.20.2 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.7.0 (gcc9_2020_q2_update) + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx and STM32WB10xx devices.
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle.
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them requires a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Known Limitations

  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_FFD_static_fw.bin and stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_RFD_static_fw.bin:
    • When using the static concurrent mode BLE/Zigbee binaries, due to a memory leak inside Zigbee shutdown procedure, the number of transitions from Zigbee to BLE is limited. This number depends on the available memory for the application. For instance, the BLE_Zigbee_Static application, available inside this package, faces this limitation after 10 transition average.
    • The workaround is to rely on the dynamic concurrent mode provided by stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_FFD_dynamic_fw.bin which is not facing this limitation.
    • This limitation will be corrected inside a future release and is referenced under ID95417.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.

  • The stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_RFD_dynamic_fw coprocessor wireless binary must be flashed only using the USB interface (as defined in the release note located in the STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries folder). It is not possible to flash this binary via ST-LINK.

  • The STM32CubeIDE/MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_DataThroughput/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/MDK-ARM
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/STM32CubeIDE
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following applications:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_ThermometerSensor/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Client_Router/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Server_Coord/STM32CubeIDE/

Main Changes

Maintenance Release for BLE, Thread and Zigbee updates

  • Thread updates
    • Introducing following new binary: stm32wb5x_Thread_RCP_fw.bin to support Thread Border Router Setup
  • BLE updates
    • Introducing BLE Basic stack with reduced features keeping following configuration:
      • GAP peripheral & Central (8 links - LL slave up to 2 links)
      • GATT server, client
      • Data length extension
      • Privacy
      • White list
      • Legacy Pairing, LE secure connections
      • HCI interface (reduced)
    • Additional beacon feature support
    • Critical code optimized in timing during execution
    • The command “ACI_GAP_START_NAME_DISCOVERY_PROC” will be deprecated on next STM32Cube_FW_WB release v1.13.0
  • Zigbee updates
    • zb_destroy_process improvement correcting some potential memory issues
    • Memory allocation improvement 
    • Power consumption improvement when using fragmentation for a sleepy end device (transfer of payload > 50 bytes)


Maintenance Release for CMSIS, HAL/LL Drivers and Projects updates

  • CMSIS Device updates
    • Update CMSIS device to include latest corrections
    • Add atomic register access services:
      • 32-bit register access: ATOMIC_SET_BIT(), ATOMIC_CLEAR_BIT(), ATOMIC_MODIFY_REG()
      • 16-bit register access: ATOMIC_SETH_BIT(), ATOMIC_CLEARH_BIT(), ATOMIC_MODIFYH_BIT()
    • Update linker files templates for all IDE (.icf/.sct/.ld)
      • RAM start address has been updated from 0x20000000/0x20000004 to 0x20000008 to be aligned on a 8 byte boundary, and be compatible with ARM Compiler 6 (Keil MDK-ARM)
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • HAL/LL Drivers updates
    • Update HAL/LL drivers to include latest corrections
      • Update of HAL CORTEX, CRYP, EXTI, FLASH, GPIO, I2C, IWDG, RCC, RTC, RNG, SMBUS, SPI, UART, USB and LL DMA, RTC, SPI, LPUART, USART drivers
      • Update of HAL SMBUS driver to introduce fast mode and fast mode plus
        • New extension files: stm32wbxx_hal_smbus_ex.h/.c for new APIs
    • Refer to release notes for further details
  • Projects updates
    • Update of FW projects following changes in latest version of HAL/LL and Middlewares
    • Templates MDK-ARM projects migrated to ARM Compiler 6 (AC-5 like warnings)
    • Update linker files templates for all IDE (.icf/.sct/.ld)
      • RAM start address has been updated from 0x20000000/0x20000004 to 0x20000008 to be aligned on a 8 byte boundary
    • Add support of new applications:
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat
      • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Lowpower
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Proximity
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Thread/Thread_RCP
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Demontrations/Audio_BVLINKWB
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_HeartRate
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_ThermometerSensor
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Sensor
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_TransparentMode
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Thread/Thread_Coap_Generic
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Client_Router
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Server_Coord
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Client_Router
      • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Server_Coord

Known Limitations

  • FUS upgrade:
    • If Anti-Rollback needs to be activated, please make sure to activate it only after installing the latest FUS version (>= V1.2.0) and after successfully installing a wireless stack (without deleting it). Otherwise, further wireless stack installation will be blocked.
  • stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_FFD_static_fw.bin and stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_RFD_static_fw.bin:
    • When using the static concurrent mode BLE/Zigbee binaries, due to a memory leak inside Zigbee shutdown procedure, the number of transitions from Zigbee to BLE is limited. This number depends on the available memory for the application. For instance, the BLE_Zigbee_Static application, available inside this package, faces this limitation after 10 transition average.
    • The workaround is to rely on the dynamic concurrent mode provided by stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_FFD_dynamic_fw.bin which is not facing this limitation.
    • This limitation will be corrected inside a future release and is referenced under ID95417.
  • Application Zigbee_Commissioning_Server_Router:
    • For STM32CubeIDE project, some elements inside the traces are not correctly displayed (uint64_t formatting only). Not observable on IAR and MDK-ARM project.

  • The stm32wb5x_BLE_Zigbee_RFD_dynamic_fw coprocessor wireless binary must be flashed only using the USB interface (as defined in the release note located in the STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries folder). It is not possible to flash this binary via ST-LINK.

  • The STM32CubeIDE/MDK-ARM projects are not available for the following applications and examples:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_DataThroughput/STM32CubeIDE
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/MDK-ARM
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Examples/BSP/STM32CubeIDE
  • The Debug configuration is not available with STM32CubeIDE projects for the following applications:
    • /NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/BLE/BLE_Ota/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Mesh_ThermometerSensor/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_Sensor/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE/BLE_p2pServer/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/BLE_LLD/BLE_LLD_Chat/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Client_Router/STM32CubeIDE/
    • /STM32WB5MM-DK/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_TempMeas_Server_Coord/STM32CubeIDE/

Development Toolchains and Compilers

  • IAR Embedded Workbench for ARM (EWARM) toolchain V8.20.2 + ST-Link
  • RealView Microcontroller Development Kit (MDK-ARM) toolchain V5.31 + ST-Link
  • STM32CubeIDE toolchain V1.7.0 + ST-Link

Supported Devices and boards

  • STM32WB55xx, STM32WB50xx, STM32WB35xx, STM32WB30xx, STM32WB15xx and STM32WB10xx devices.
  • P-NUCLEO-WB55 kit composed of P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo and P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle.
  • STM32WB5MM-DK board
  • NUCLEO-WB15CC board

Dependencies

This software release is compatible with:

  • STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries available under Projects/STM32WB_Copro_Wireless_Binaries

Several applications (BLE (Bluetooth low energy), Thread or Mac 802-15-4) are available under:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications

All of them are provided in source code and some of them are also available in binary format directly for ready to use usage:

  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/P-NUCLEO-WB55.USBDongle/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex
  • Projects/NUCLEO-WB15CC/Applications/xxx/Binary/.hex

Each of them require a different coprocessor binary in order to behave correctly. This is documented inside each readme.txt of those applications.

For a detailed explanation on how to use and how to flash them, you can refer to:

  • release note for STM32WB5x
  • release note for STM32WB3x
  • release note for STM32WB1x

Main Changes

Patch Release for FUS security update and Wireless protocols corrections

  • FUS:
    • Add functional security enhancements
  • BLE:
    • STM32WB15/WB10 VCO settings update to enhance RX path
    • Data throughput enhancement on all projects
    • Ability to reconnect in secure mode on a 2nd link if master database is clear during 1st link connection
    • Resolution of ACI_GAP_BOND_LOST_Event timeout in case Allow_rebond is not sent
    • PTS issue ticket done CASE0070853: destination channel ID value above 1000 should be allowed and test passed
    • BLE_Ota application improved to be SBSFU ready and support Flash driver use / SEM7 flash activity control
  • Thread:
    • Power consumption enhancement when running above 3mn in Thread_SED_Coap_Multicast example   
  • Zigbee:
    • Allow Zigbee stack to go in low power mode after SF timer wrap-around
    • Add support of 2 new Zigbee FreeRTOS example applications (IAR only):
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Client_Router_FreeRTOS
      • /P-NUCLEO-WB55.Nucleo/Applications/Zigbee/Zigbee_OnOff_Server_Coord_FreeRTOS  
  • MAC 802.15.4:
    • Allow the user to set the PLL @64MHz for CM4
